10. command=generate_image;text_prompt={text}

To use a specific tool, you should ask all necessary questions to gather the required data. Once you have all the data, you should respond with the selected command and input arguments based on the data received. If there is no api command available you should answer "I don't know".
USER: Convert the text "Hello World" to speech.
OTHER: To convert the text to speech, I need to know the language and the gender of the voice. Could you please provide these details?
USER: en
OTHER: You have provided the language code, but I still need the gender of the voice. Could you please provide this information?
USER: english, en
OTHER: I understand the language is English, but I still need the gender of the voice. Could you please specify if you want a male or female voice?
USER: fmale
OTHER: command=convert_text_to_speech;text=Hello World;language_code=en;gender=female

8. command=get_news;country={country};date={date}
9. command=convert_text_to_speech;text={text};language_code={language_code};gender={gender}
10. command=generate_image;text_prompt={text}

To use a specific tool, you should ask all necessary questions to gather the required data. Once you have all the data, you should respond with the selected command and input arguments based on the data received. If there is no api command available you should answer "I don't know".
USER: Can I get the latest news about technology in the United States?
OTHER: I'm sorry, but the current API commands do not support fetching news based on a specific topic like technology. However, you can get the latest news from a specific country. Would you like to proceed with that?
USER: new york
OTHER: I'm sorry for the confusion, but could you please clarify your request? Are you asking for the weather in New York, news from New York, or something else?
USER: yes
OTHER: I'm sorry, but your response is still unclear. Are you asking for the weather in New York or news from New York?
USER: news
OTHER: To get the latest news from New York, United States, you can use the following API command:

command=get_news;country=United States;date={date}

Please replace {date} with the current date in the format YYYY-MM-DD.
USER: 2023-12-01
OTHER: Here is the API command to get the news from New York, United States on December 1, 2023:

command=get_news;country=United States;date=2023-12-01
